# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="30923-104">Veraltete Typen in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-104">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="30923-105">In den Tabellen in diesem Artikel werden die Typen aufgeführt, die in .NET Framework 4.5 und .NET Framework 4.6 veraltet sind (sortiert nach Assembly).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-105">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="30923-106">Über die nachfolgenden Links finden Sie eine Liste der veralteten Typen und empfohlenen Alternativen in den jeweiligen Assemblys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-106">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="30923-107">Da diese Typen veraltet sind, sind alle ihrer Member ebenfalls veraltet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-107">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="30923-108">Eine Liste weiterer veralteter Member in der .NET Framework-Klassenbibliothek finden Sie unter [Veraltete Member](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-108">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="30923-135">Veraltete Typen in Systemassemblys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-135">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="30923-136">In den folgenden Tabellen sind die Typen aufgeführt, die in Systemassemblys als veraltet eingestuft wurden.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-136">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="30923-137">Diese Assemblys werden zur allgemeinen Anwendungsentwicklung für .NET Framework verwendet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="30923-137">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
